Cavolini Regular (cavolini.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Cavolini', Everything looks good.

Pass

Please verify against spec. It should follow this structure:
'Copyright (c) XXXX - XXXX /entity/. All rights reserved.'

Cavolini Italic (cavolini-italic.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Cavolini-Italic', Everything looks good.

Please verify against job spec.
MS NID 13 is:
You may use this font as permitted by the EULA for the product in which this font is included to display and print content. You may only (i) embed this font in content as permitted by the embedding restrictions included in this font; and (ii) temporarily download this font to a printer or other output device to help print content. This web font file is intended for use with the Microsoft Sway application only, and not for further use or distribution of any kind.

This font software is the property of Monotype Imaging Inc., or one of its affiliated entities (collectively, Monotype) and its use by you is covered under the terms of a license agreement. You have obtained this font software either directly from Monotype or together with software distributed by one of the licensees of Monotype. This software is a valuable asset of Monotype. Unless you have entered into a specific license agreement granting you additional rights, your use of this software is limited by the terms of the actual license agreement you have entered into with Monotype. You may not copy or distribute this software. If you have any questions concerning your rights you should review the license agreement you received with the software. You can learn more about Monotype by clicking here: www.monotype.com.

, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Cavolini-Bold', Everything looks good.

Cavolini Bold Italic (cavolini-bolditalic.ttf)

name

Mac NID 6

Mac NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Cavolini-BoldItalic', Everything looks good.

Pass

name

MS NID 0

MS NID 0, Copyright.

There is something wrong:
'Copyright © 2015, 2016 Monotype Imaging Inc. All rights reserved'
Please verify against spec. It should follow this structure:
'Copyright (c) XXXX - XXXX /entity/. All rights reserved.'

PostScript names

Cavolini Regular (cavolini.ttf)

post

PostScript names

Postscript names should not be longer then 29 characters. May cause issues in PDF.

Every PostScript name is fine.
